Utah Code Annotated - Title 17C - Limited Purpose Local Government Entities - Community Reinvestment Agency Act
===============================================================================================================

Utah Code Annotated - Title 17C - Chapter 1 - Agency Operations
***************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-101(1): This title is known as the "Limited Purpose Local Government Entities - Community Reinvestment Agency Act."
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-101(2): This chapter is known as "Agency Operations."
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-101(3): This part is known as "General Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this title:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(1): 17C-1-702 "Active project area" means a project area that has not been dissolved in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(2): 17C-1-403; 17C-1-403(3); 17C-1-404; 17C-1-406 "Adjusted tax increment" means  the percentage of tax increment, if less than 100%, that an agency is authorized to receive:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(2)(a): 17C-1-403; 17C-1-403(3) for a pre-July 1, 1993, project area plan, under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(2)(b): 17C-1-404; 17C-1-406 for a post-June 30, 1993, project area plan, under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(2)(c): under a project area budget approved by a taxing entity committee; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(2)(d): under an interlocal agreement that authorizes the agency to receive a taxing entity's tax increment.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(3): "Affordable housing" means housing owned or occupied by a low or moderate income family, as determined by resolution of the agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4): 17C-1-201.5 "Agency" or "community reinvestment agency" means a separate body corporate and politic, created under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4)(a): that is a political subdivision of the state;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4)(b): that is created to undertake or promote project area development as provided in this title; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4)(c): whose geographic boundaries are coterminous with:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4)(c)(i): for an agency created by a county, the unincorporated area of the county; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(4)(c)(ii): for an agency created by a municipality, the boundaries of the municipality.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(5): 17C-1-1001; 17C-1-1001; 17C-1-1001; 17C-1-1001 "Agency funds" means money that an agency collects or receives for agency operations, implementing a project area plan or an implementation plan as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(5)(a): project area funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(5)(b): 17C-1-1001 income, proceeds, revenue, or property derived from or held in connection with the agency's undertaking and implementation of project area development or agency-wide project development as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(5)(c): a contribution, loan, grant, or other financial assistance from any public or private source;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(5)(d): 17C-1-1001 project area incremental revenue as defined in Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(8): "Base taxable value" means, unless otherwise adjusted in accordance with provisions of this title, a property's taxable value as shown upon the assessment roll last equalized during the base year.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9): 17C-1-402(4)(c) "Base year" means, except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(a): for a pre-July 1, 1993, urban renewal or economic development project area plan, before the project area plan's effective date;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(b): for a post-June 30, 1993, urban renewal or economic development project area plan, or a community reinvestment project area plan that is subject to a taxing entity committee:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(b)(i): before the date on which the taxing entity committee approves the project area budget; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(b)(ii): if taxing entity committee approval is not required for the project area budget, before the date on which the community legislative body adopts the project area plan;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(c)(i): the date on which the inactive airport site is sold for remediation and development; or

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(9)(d): for a community development project area plan or a community reinvestment project area plan that is subject to an interlocal agreement, as described in the interlocal agreement.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(15): "Community" means a county or municipality.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(25): "Family" means the same as that term is defined in regulations of the United States Department of Housing and Urban Development, 24 C.F.R. Section 5.403, as amended or as superseded by replacement regulations.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(27): "Hazardous waste" means any substance defined, regulated, or listed as a hazardous substance, hazardous material, hazardous waste, toxic waste, pollutant, contaminant, or toxic substance, or identified as hazardous to human health or the environment, under state or federal law or regulation.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(32): "Income targeted housing" means housing that is owned or occupied by a family whose annual income is at or below 80% of the median annual income for a family within the county in which the housing is located.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(33): "Incremental value" means a figure derived by multiplying the marginal value of the property located within a project area on which tax increment is collected by a number that represents the adjusted tax increment from that project area that is paid to the agency.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(44): "Pre-July 1, 1993, project area plan" means a project area plan adopted before July 1, 1993, whether or not amended subsequent to the project area plan's adoption.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(46): "Project area" means the geographic area described in a project area plan within which the project area development described in the project area plan takes place or is proposed to take place.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(47): 17C-2-201; 17C-3-201; 17C-4-204; 17C-5-302 "Project area budget" means a multiyear projection of annual or cumulative revenues and expenses and other fiscal matters pertaining to a project area prepared in accordance with:

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(48)(a): promoting, creating, or retaining public or private jobs within the state or a community;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102(48)(b): providing office, manufacturing, warehousing, distribution, parking, or other facilities or improvements;

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Beginning on May 10, 2016, an agency:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(1): Chapter 5, Community Reinvestment may create a community reinvestment project area under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(2): (3); Chapter 2, Urban Renewal; Chapter 3, Economic Development; Chapter 4, Community Development except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(2)(a): Chapter 2, Urban Renewal an urban renewal project area under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(2)(b): Chapter 3, Economic Development an economic development project area under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(2)(c): Chapter 4, Community Development a community development project area under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(3): 17C-2-101.5; 17C-3-101.5; 17C-4-101.5 may create an urban renewal project area, an economic development project area, or a community development project area if:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(3)(a): 17C-2-101.5; 17C-3-101.5; 17C-4-101.5 before April 1, 2016, the agency adopts a resolution in accordance with:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-102.5(3)(a)(i): 17C-2-101.5 Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103 Limitations on applicability of title -- Amendment of previously adopted project area plan.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1): Except where expressly provided, nothing in this title may be construed to:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(a): impose a requirement or obligation on an agency, with respect to a project area plan adopted or an agency action taken, that was not imposed by the law in effect at the time the project area plan was adopted or the action taken;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(b): prohibit an agency from taking an action that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(b)(i): was allowed by the law in effect immediately before an applicable amendment to this title;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(b)(ii): is permitted or required under the project area plan adopted before the amendment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(b)(iii): is not explicitly prohibited under this title;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(c): revive any right to challenge any action of the agency that had already expired; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(1)(d): require a project area plan to contain a provision that was not required by the law in effect at the time the project area plan was adopted.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-103(2): (2)(a)

----------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1): Part 10, Agency Taxing Authority An agency may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(a): sue and be sued;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(g): provide for project area development as provided in this title;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(h): receive and use agency funds as provided in this title;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(j): accept financial or other assistance from any public or private source for the agency's activities, powers, and duties, and expend any funds the agency receives for any purpose described in this title;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(k): borrow money or accept financial or other assistance from a public entity or any other source for any of the purposes of this title and comply with any conditions of any loan or assistance;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(l): issue bonds to finance the undertaking of any project area development or for any of the agency's other purposes, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(l)(i): reimbursing an advance made by the agency or by a public entity to the agency;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(l)(ii): refunding bonds to pay or retire bonds previously issued by the agency; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(l)(iii): refunding bonds to pay or retire bonds previously issued by the community that created the agency for expenses associated with project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(m): pay an impact fee, exaction, or other fee imposed by a community in connection with land development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(n): Part 10, Agency Taxing Authority subject to
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-202(1)(o): transact other business and exercise all other powers described in this title.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203 Agency board -- Quorum.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(1): The governing body of an agency is a board consisting of the current members of the community legislative body.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(2): A majority of board members constitutes a quorum for the transaction of agency business.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(3): A board may not adopt a resolution, pass a motion, or take any other official board action without the concurrence of at least a majority of the board members present at a meeting at which a quorum is present.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4): 10-3b-102; 17-52a-203
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(a): 10-3b-102 The mayor or the mayor's designee of a municipality operating under a council-mayor form of government, as defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(a)(i): serves as the executive director of an agency created by the municipality; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(a)(ii): exercises the agency's executive powers.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(b): 17-52a-203 The county executive or the county executive's designee of a county operating under a county executive-council form of government, as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(b)(i): serves as the executive director of an agency created by the county; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-203(4)(b)(ii): exercises the agency's executive powers.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204 Project area development by an adjoining agency -- Requirements.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(1)(a): A community, regardless of whether the community has created an agency, may enter into an interlocal agreement with an agency located in the same or an abutting county that authorizes the agency to exercise all the powers granted to an agency under this title within all or a portion of the community.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(1)(b): (1)(a) The agency and the community shall adopt an interlocal agreement described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(2): (1) If an agency and a community enter into an interlocal agreement under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(2)(a): the agency may act in all respects as if a project area within the community were within the agency's boundaries;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(2)(b): the board has all the rights, powers, and privileges with respect to a project area within the community as if the project area were within the agency's boundaries;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(2)(c): the agency may be paid project area funds to the same extent as if a project area within the community were within the agency's boundaries; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(2)(d): the community legislative body shall adopt, by ordinance, each project area plan within the community approved by the agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(3): If an agency's project area abuts another agency's project area, the agencies may coordinate with each other in order to assist and cooperate in the planning, undertaking, construction, or operation of project area development located within each agency's project area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(4)(a)(i): "County agency" means an agency that is created by a county.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(4)(a)(ii): 10-1-104 "Industrial property" means private real property:

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-204(4)(a)(ii)(B): comprises some or all of an inactive industrial site.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205 Transfer of project area from one community to another.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1): As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(a): "New agency" means the agency created by the new community.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(b): "New community" means the community in which the relocated project area is located after the change in community boundaries takes place.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(c): "Original agency" means the agency created by the original community.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(d): "Original community" means the community that adopted the project area plan that created the project area that has been relocated.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(e): "Relocated" means that a project area under a project area plan adopted by the original community has ceased to be located within that community and has become part of a new community because of a change in community boundaries through:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(e)(i): a county or municipal annexation;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(e)(ii): the creation of a new county;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(e)(iii): a municipal incorporation, consolidation, dissolution, or boundary adjustment; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(1)(e)(iv): any other action resulting in a change in community boundaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-205(2): A relocated project area shall, for purposes of this title, be considered to remain in the original community until the original agency and the new agency enter into an interlocal agreement, adopted by resolution of the original agency's and the new agency's board, that authorizes the original agency to transfer or assign to the new agency the original agency's real property, rights, indebtedness, obligations, tax increment, or other assets and liabilities resulting from the relocated project area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-208 Agency funds.
---------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-208(1): Agency funds shall be accounted for separately from the funds of the community that created the agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-208(2): An agency may accumulate retained earnings or fund balances, as appropriate, in any fund.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-209 Agency records.
-----------------------------------------------
An agency shall maintain the agency's minutes, resolutions, and other records separate from those of the community that created the agency.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-415 Obligations of agencies that use tax increment to pay for communication infrastructure or facility.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
An agency that uses tax increment on or after March 30, 2009 to pay for communication infrastructure or a communication facility:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-415(1): may not make or grant any undue or unreasonable preference or advantage to a provider of communication service with respect to the communication infrastructure or communication facility for which the tax increment is used; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-415(2): shall allow the communication infrastructure and facilities for which tax increment is used to be used by any other provider of communication service on a fair, equitable, and nondiscriminatory basis.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.1 Title.
----------------------------------------
This part is known as "Agency Bonds."

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.5 Resolution authorizing issuance of agency bonds -- Characteristics of bonds.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.5(1): An agency may not issue a bond under this part unless the board first adopts a resolution authorizing the bond issuance.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.5(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.5(2)(a): As provided in the agency resolution authorizing the issuance of a bond under this part or the trust indenture under which the bond is issued, a bond issued under this part may be issued in one or more series and may be sold at public or private sale and in the manner provided in the resolution or indenture.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-501.5(2)(b): A bond issued by an agency under this part shall bear the date, be payable at the time, bear interest at the rate, be in the denomination and in the form, carry the conversion or registration privileges, have the rank or priority, be executed in the manner, be subject to the terms of redemption or tender, with or without premium, be payable in the medium of payment and at the place, and have other characteristics as provided in the agency resolution authorizing the bond issuance or the trust indenture under which the bond is issued.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502 Sources from which bonds may be made payable -- Agency powers regarding bonds.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1): 17C-1-1001; (1)(a); (g) An agency may pay the principal and interest on a bond issued by the agency from:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(a): the income and revenues of the project area development financed with the proceeds of the bond;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(b): the income and revenue of certain designated project area development regardless of whether the project area development is financed in whole or in part with the proceeds of the bond;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(c): the income, proceeds, revenue, property, or agency funds derived from or held in connection with the agency's undertaking and implementation of project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(d): project area funds;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(e): agency revenues generally;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(f): a contribution, loan, grant, or other financial assistance from a public entity in aid of project area development, including the assignment of revenue or taxes in support of an agency bond;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(g): 17C-1-1001 project area incremental revenue or property tax revenue as those terms are defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(1)(h): (1)(a); (g) funds derived from any combination of the methods listed in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2): In connection with the issuance of an agency bond, an agency may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2)(a): pledge all or any part of the agency's gross or net rents, fees, or revenues to which the agency's right then exists or may thereafter come into existence;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2)(b): encumber by mortgage, deed of trust, or otherwise all or any part of the agency's real or personal property, then owned or thereafter acquired; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2)(c): make the covenants and take the action that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2)(c)(i): may be necessary, convenient, or desirable to secure the bond; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-502(2)(c)(ii): except as otherwise provided in this chapter, will tend to make the bond more marketable, even though such covenants or actions are not specifically enumerated in this chapter.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-503 Signature of officer who leaves office.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
If an agency officer whose signature appears on a bond issued under this part leaves office before delivery of the bond, the signature shall continue to be valid as if the official had remained in office until delivery of the bond.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504 Contesting the legality of resolution authorizing bonds -- Time limit -- Presumption.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(1): 11-14-316(2) Any person may contest the legality of the resolution authorizing issuance of the bond or any provisions for the security and payment of the bond for a period of 30 days after:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(1)(a): publication of the resolution authorizing the bond; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(1)(b): 11-14-316(2) publication of a notice of bond containing substantially the items required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(2): (1) After the 30-day period described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(3): In a lawsuit or other proceeding involving the question of whether a bond issued under this part is valid or enforceable or involving the security for a bond, if a bond recites that the agency issued the bond in connection with project area development:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(3)(a): the bond shall be conclusively presumed to have been issued for that purpose; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-504(3)(b): the project area plan and project area shall be conclusively presumed to have been properly formed, adopted, planned, located, and implemented in accordance with this title.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-505 Authority to purchase agency bonds.
-------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-505(1): Any person, firm, corporation, association, political subdivision of the state, or other entity or public or private officer may purchase a bond issued by an agency under this part with funds owned or controlled by the purchaser.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-505(2): Nothing in this section may be construed to relieve a purchaser of an agency bond of any duty to exercise reasonable care in selecting securities.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506 Those executing bonds not personally liable -- Limitation of obligations under bonds -- Negotiability.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(1): A member of a board or other person executing an agency bond is not liable personally on the bond.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(2): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(2)(a): A bond issued by an agency is not a general obligation or liability of the community, the state, or any of the state's political subdivisions and does not constitute a charge against their general credit or taxing powers.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(2)(b): A bond issued by an agency is not payable out of any funds or properties other than those of the agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(2)(c): The community, the state, and the state's political subdivisions may not be liable on a bond issued by an agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(2)(d): A bond issued by an agency does not constitute indebtedness within the meaning of any constitutional or statutory debt limitation.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-506(3): A bond issued by an agency under this part is fully negotiable.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507 Obligee rights -- Board may confer other rights.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(1): In addition to all other rights that are conferred on an obligee of a bond issued by an agency under this part and subject to contractual restrictions binding on the obligee, an obligee may:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(1)(a): by mandamus, suit, action, or other proceeding, compel an agency and the agency's board, officers, agents, or employees to perform every term, provision, and covenant contained in any contract of the agency with or for the benefit of the obligee, and require the agency to carry out the covenants and agreements of the agency and to fulfill all duties imposed on the agency by this part; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(1)(b): by suit, action, or other proceeding, enjoin any acts or things that may be unlawful or violate the rights of the obligee.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2): (2)(b); (2)(a); (2)(b)(i)(B)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(a): (2)(b) In a board resolution authorizing the issuance of a bond or in a trust indenture, mortgage, lease, or other contract, a board may confer upon an obligee holding or representing a specified amount in bonds, the rights described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b): (2)(a); (2)(b)(i)(B)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(i): (2)(a) The rights that the board may confer under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(i)(A): cause possession of all or part of the project area development to be surrendered to an obligee;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(i)(B): obtain the appointment of a receiver of all or part of an agency's project area development and of the rents and profits from the project area development; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(i)(C): require the agency and the board and employees to account as if the agency and the board and employees were the trustees of an express trust.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(ii): (2)(b)(i)(B) If a receiver is appointed through the exercise of a right granted under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(ii)(A): may enter and take possession of the project area development or any part of the project area development, operate and maintain the project area development, and collect and receive all fees, rents, revenues, or other charges arising from the project area development after the receiver's appointment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-507(2)(b)(ii)(B): shall keep money collected as receiver for the agency in a separate account and apply the money pursuant to the agency obligations as the court directs.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-508 Bonds exempt from taxes -- Agency may purchase an agency's own bonds.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-508(1): A bond issued by an agency under this part is issued for an essential public and governmental purpose and is, together with interest on the bond and income from it, exempt from all state taxes except the corporate franchise tax.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-508(2): An agency may purchase the agency's own bonds at a price that the board determines.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-508(3): Nothing in this section may be construed to limit the right of an obligee to pursue a remedy for the enforcement of a pledge or lien given under this part by an agency on the agency's rents, fees, grants, properties, or revenues.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.1 Title.
----------------------------------------
This part is known as "Agency Annual Report, Budget, and Audit Requirements."

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5 Annual agency budget -- Fiscal year -- Public hearing required -- Notice -- Auditor forms -- Requirement to file form.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(1): Each agency shall prepare an annual budget of the agency's revenues and expenditures for each fiscal year.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(2): The board shall adopt each agency budget:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(2)(a): for an agency created by a municipality, before June 30; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(2)(b): for an agency created by a county, before December 15.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(3): The agency's fiscal year shall be the same as the fiscal year of the community that created the agency.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(4): 63G-30-102
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(4)(a): Before adopting an annual budget, each board shall hold a public hearing on the annual budget.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(4)(c): Each agency shall make the annual budget available for public inspection at least three days before the date of the public hearing.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(5): The state auditor shall prescribe the budget forms and the categories to be contained in each annual budget, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(5)(a): revenues and expenditures for the budget year;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(5)(b): legal fees; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(5)(c): administrative costs, including rent, supplies, and other materials, and salaries of agency personnel.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(6): (6)(a)

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-601.5(6)(b): (6)(a) The requirement of Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-607 State Tax Commission and county assessor required to account for new growth.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Upon the expiration of a project area funds collection period, the State Tax Commission and the assessor of each county in which a project area is located shall count as new growth the assessed value of property with respect to which the taxing entity is receiving taxes or increased taxes for the first time.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-609 Agency reporting limitations.
-------------------------------------------------------------
Except as required under this title, an agency is not required to submit to a public entity information or a report related to the agency's operations or project areas.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-905 Court award for court costs and attorney fees, relocation expenses, and damage to fixtures or personal property.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-905(2)(b): a party conducting a business on the acquired property; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-905(2)(c): Title 57, Chapter 12, Utah Relocation Assistance Act a person displaced from the property, as permitted by
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-905(3): an amount to compensate for any fixtures or personal property that is:

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-905(3)(b): damaged as a result of the acquisition or relocation.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001 Definitions.
---------------------------------------------
As used in this part:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(1)(a): "Agency-wide project development" means activity within the agency's boundaries that, as determined by the board, encourages, promotes, or provides development or redevelopment for the purpose of achieving the results described in an implementation plan, including affordable housing.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(1)(b): "Agency-wide project development" does not include project area development under a project area plan.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(2): 59-2-924 "Certified tax rate" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(3): "Cooperative development project" means project area development with impacts that extend beyond an agency's geographic boundaries to the benefit of two or more communities.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(4): Title 63N, Economic Opportunity Act "Economic development project" means project area development for the purpose of:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(4)(a): creating, developing, attracting, and retaining business;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(4)(b): creating or preserving jobs;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(4)(c): stimulating business and economic activity; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(4)(d): Title 63N, Economic Opportunity Act providing a local incentive as required by the Governor's Office of Economic Opportunity under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(5): "Eligible taxing entity" means a taxing entity that:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(5)(a): is a municipality, a county, or a school district; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(5)(b): contains an agency partially or completely within the taxing entity's geographic boundaries.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(6): 17C-1-1004 "Implementation plan" means a plan adopted in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(6)(a): describes how the agency uses property tax revenue; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(6)(b): guides and controls agency-wide project development.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(7): "Project area incremental revenue" means the amount of revenue generated by the incremental value that a taxing entity receives after a project area funds collection period ends.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-1-1001(8): "Property tax revenue" means the amount of revenue generated by an agency from the property within the agency using the current taxable value of the property and the agency's certified tax rate.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-101.1 Title.
----------------------------------------
This chapter is known as "Urban Renewal."

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-101.2 Applicability of chapter.
-----------------------------------------------------------
This chapter applies to an urban renewal project area that is effective:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-101.2(1): before May 10, 2016; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-101.2(2): 17C-2-101.5 before September 1, 2016, if an agency adopted a resolution in accordance with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-101.5(1)(c): contains a boundary description or map of the survey area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103 Urban renewal project area plan requirements.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1): 17C-1-414; (2); 9-8a-404 An agency shall ensure that each urban renewal project area plan and proposed project area plan:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(a): 17C-1-414 describes the boundaries of the project area, subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(b): contains a general statement of the land uses, layout of principal streets, population densities, and building intensities of the project area and how they will be affected by the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(c): states the standards that will guide the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(d): shows how the purposes of this title will be attained by the project area development;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(f): describes how the project area development will reduce or eliminate a development impediment in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(g): describes any specific project or projects that are the object of the proposed project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(h): identifies how a participant will be selected to undertake the project area development and identify each participant currently involved in the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(i): states the reasons for the selection of the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(j): describes the physical, social, and economic conditions existing in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(k): describes any tax incentives offered private entities for facilities located in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(l): (2) includes the analysis described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(m): 9-8a-404 if any of the existing buildings or uses in the project area are included in or eligible for inclusion in the National Register of Historic Places or the State Register, states that the agency shall comply with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(1)(n): includes other information that the agency determines to be necessary or advisable.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2): (1)(l) An agency shall ensure that each analysis under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2)(a): the benefit of any financial assistance or other public subsidy proposed to be provided by the agency, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2)(a)(i): an evaluation of the reasonableness of the costs of the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2)(a)(ii): efforts the agency or participant has made or will make to maximize private investment;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2)(a)(iv): an estimate of the total amount of tax increment that will be expended in undertaking project area development and the project area funds collection period; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-103(2)(b): the anticipated public benefit to be derived from the project area development, including:

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-104 Existing and historic buildings and uses in an urban renewal project area.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
If any of the existing buildings or uses in an urban renewal project area are included in or eligible for inclusion in the National Register of Historic Places or the State Register, the agency shall comply with Section

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-105 Objections to urban renewal project area plan -- Owners' alternative project area plan -- Election if 40% of property owners object.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-105(1): At any time before the plan hearing, any person may file with the agency a written statement of objections to the proposed urban renewal project area plan.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-302 Development impediment hearing -- Owners may review evidence of a development impediment.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-302(1)(b)(ii): present evidence and testimony, including expert testimony, concerning the existence or nonexistence of a development impediment.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-302(2): The agency shall allow record owners of property located within a proposed urban renewal project area the opportunity, for at least 30 days before the hearing, to review the evidence of a development impediment compiled by the agency or by the person or firm conducting the development impediment study for the agency, including any expert report.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303 Conditions on board determination of a development impediment -- Conditions of a development impediment caused by the participant.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1): 17C-2-102(1)(a)(ii)(B); (1)(a)(iv) A board may not make a development impediment determination in a resolution under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a): (1)(a)(iv)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(i): the proposed project area consists predominantly of nongreenfield parcels;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(ii): the proposed project area is currently zoned for urban purposes and generally served by utilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iii): at least 50% of the parcels within the proposed project area contain nonagricultural or nonaccessory buildings or improvements used or intended for residential, commercial, industrial, or other urban purposes, or any combination of those uses;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv): the present condition or use of the proposed project area substantially impairs the sound growth of the municipality, retards the provision of housing accommodations, or constitutes an economic liability or is detrimental to the public health, safety, or welfare, as shown by the existence within the proposed project area of at least four of the following factors:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(A): one of the following, although sometimes interspersed with well maintained buildings and infrastructure:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(A)(I): substantial physical dilapidation, deterioration, or defective construction of buildings or infrastructure; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(A)(II): significant noncompliance with current building code, safety code, health code, or fire code requirements or local ordinances;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(B): unsanitary or unsafe conditions in the proposed project area that threaten the health, safety, or welfare of the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(C): environmental hazards, as defined in state or federal law, that require remediation as a condition for current or future use and development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(D): excessive vacancy, abandoned buildings, or vacant lots within an area zoned for urban use and served by utilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(E): abandoned or outdated facilities that pose a threat to public health, safety, or welfare;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(F): criminal activity in the project area, higher than that of comparable areas in the municipality or county that are without a development impediment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(iv)(G): defective or unusual conditions of title rendering the title nonmarketable; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(v): (1)(a)(iv)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(v)(A): (1)(a)(iv) at least 50% of the privately-owned parcels within the proposed project area are affected by at least one of the factors, but not necessarily the same factor, listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(a)(v)(B): the affected parcels comprise at least 66% of the privately-owned acreage of the proposed project area; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(1)(b): the proposed project area includes some or all of a superfund site, inactive industrial site, or inactive airport site.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-2-303(2): (1)(a)(iii); (iv) No single parcel comprising 10% or more of the acreage of the proposed project area may be counted as satisfying Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-102(1)(f)(i): the oral and written objections to the proposed project area plan and evidence and testimony for or against adoption of the proposed project area plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-102(1)(f)(ii): whether to revise, approve, or reject the proposed project area plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-102(1)(g): 17C-3-105 approve the proposed project area plan, with or without revisions, as the project area plan by a resolution that complies with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-102(1)(h): submit the project area plan to the community legislative body for adoption.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103 Economic development project area plan requirements.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1): 17C-1-414; (2); 9-8a-404(1) Each economic development project area plan and proposed project area plan shall:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(a): 17C-1-414 describe the boundaries of the project area, subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(b): contain a general statement of the land uses, layout of principal streets, population densities, and building intensities of the project area and how they will be affected by the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(c): state the standards that will guide the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(d): show how the purposes of this title will be attained by the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(e): be consistent with the general plan of the community in which the project area is located and show that the project area development will conform to the community's general plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(f): describe how the project area development will create additional jobs;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(g): describe any specific project or projects that are the object of the proposed project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(h): identify how a participant will be selected to undertake the project area development and identify each participant currently involved in the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(i): state the reasons for the selection of the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(j): describe the physical, social, and economic conditions existing in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(k): describe any tax incentives offered private entities for facilities located in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(l): (2) include an analysis, as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(m): 9-8a-404(1) if any of the existing buildings or uses in the project area are included in or eligible for inclusion in the National Register of Historic Places or the State Register, state that the agency shall comply with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(1)(n): include other information that the agency determines to be necessary or advisable.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2): (1)(l) Each analysis under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(a): the benefit of any financial assistance or other public subsidy proposed to be provided by the agency, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(a)(i): an evaluation of the reasonableness of the costs of project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(a)(ii): efforts the agency or participant has made or will make to maximize private investment;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(a)(iii): the rationale for use of tax increment, including an analysis of whether the proposed project area development might reasonably be expected to occur in the foreseeable future solely through private investment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(a)(iv): an estimate of the total amount of tax increment that will be expended in undertaking project area development and the length of time for which it will be expended; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(b): the anticipated public benefit to be derived from the project area development, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(b)(i): the beneficial influences upon the tax base of the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(b)(ii): the associated business and economic activity likely to be stimulated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-3-103(2)(b)(iii): the number of jobs or employment anticipated to be generated or preserved.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103 Community development project area plan requirements.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Each community development project area plan and proposed project area plan shall:Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(1): 17C-1-414 describe the boundaries of the project area, subject to Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(2): contain a general statement of the land uses, layout of principal streets, population densities, and building intensities of the project area and how they will be affected by the community development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(3): state the standards that will guide the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(4): show how the purposes of this title will be attained by the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(5): be consistent with the general plan of the community in which the project area is located and show that the project area development will conform to the community's general plan;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(6): describe any specific project or projects that are the object of the proposed project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(7): identify how a participant will be selected to undertake the project area development and identify each participant currently involved in the project area development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(8): state the reasons for the selection of the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(9): describe the physical, social, and economic conditions existing in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(10): describe any tax incentives offered private entities for facilities located in the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(11): include an analysis or description of the anticipated public benefit to be derived from the project area development, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(11)(a): the beneficial influences upon the tax base of the community; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(11)(b): the associated business and economic activity likely to be stimulated; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-103(12): include other information that the agency determines to be necessary or advisable.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-104(2): the agency's purposes and intent with respect to the project area;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-104(3): the project area plan incorporated by reference; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-104(4): 17C-4-103(11) the board findings and determinations that adoption of the community development project area plan will:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-104(4)(a): satisfy a public purpose;

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204 Adoption of a budget for a community development project area plan -- Amendment.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204(1): An agency may prepare and, by resolution adopted at a regular or special meeting of the board, adopt a community development project area budget setting forth:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204(1)(a): the anticipated costs, including administrative costs, of implementing the community development project area plan; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204(1)(b): the tax increment, sales and use tax revenue, and other revenue the agency anticipates receiving to fund the project.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204(3): Each resolution to adopt or amend a budget under this section shall appear as an item on the agenda for the regular or special board meeting at which the resolution is adopted without additional required notice.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-4-204(4): An agency is not required to obtain taxing entity or taxing entity committee approval to adopt or amend a community development project area budget.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-305(5): each taxing entity affected by the agency's collection of project area funds under the community reinvestment project area budget.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-401 Title.
--------------------------------------
This part is known as " Development Impediment Determination in a Community Reinvestment Project Area."

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402 Development impediment determination in a community reinvestment project area -- Prerequisites -- Restrictions.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(1): Chapter 1, Part 9, Eminent Domain An agency shall comply with the provisions of this section before the agency may use eminent domain to acquire property under
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2): 17C-5-103; 17C-5-403; Chapter 1, Part 8, Hearing and Notice Requirements An agency shall, after adopting a survey area resolution as described in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2)(a): 17C-5-403 cause a development impediment study to be conducted within the survey area in accordance with Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2)(b): Chapter 1, Part 8, Hearing and Notice Requirements provide notice and hold a development impediment hearing in accordance with
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2)(c): after the development impediment hearing, at the same or at a subsequent meeting:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2)(c)(i): consider the evidence and information relating to the existence or nonexistence of a development impediment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-402(2)(c)(ii): by resolution, make a determination regarding whether a development impediment exists in all or part of the survey area.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(b)(i)(A): exist in part or all of the survey area; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(b)(i)(B): meet the qualifications for a development impediment determination in all or part of the survey area; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(b)(ii): whether the survey area contains all or part of a superfund site;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(c): 17C-5-405 includes a written report that states:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(c)(i): the conclusions reached;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(c)(ii): 17C-5-405 any area within the survey area that meets the statutory criteria of a development impediment under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(c)(iii): any other information requested by the agency to determine whether a development impediment exists within the survey area; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-403(1)(d): is completed within one year after the day on which the survey area resolution is adopted.

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404 Development impediment hearing -- Owners may review evidence of a development impediment.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(1): 17C-5-402(2)(b) In a hearing required under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(1)(a): permit all evidence of the existence or nonexistence of a development impediment within the survey area to be presented; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(1)(b): permit each record owner of property located within the survey area or the record property owner's representative the opportunity to:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(1)(b)(i): examine and cross-examine each witness that provides evidence of the existence or nonexistence of a development impediment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(1)(b)(ii): present evidence and testimony, including expert testimony, concerning the existence or nonexistence of a development impediment.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-404(2): An agency shall allow each record owner of property located within a survey area the opportunity, for at least 30 days before the day on which the hearing takes place, to review the evidence of a development impediment compiled by the agency or by the person or firm conducting the development impediment study for the agency, including any expert report.


Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405 Conditions on a development impediment determination -- Conditions of a development impediment caused by a participant.
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1): 17C-5-402(2)(c)(ii); (1)(a)(iv); 19-6-102 A board may not make a development impediment determination in a resolution under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a): (1)(a)(iv)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(i): the survey area consists predominantly of nongreenfield parcels;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(ii): the survey area is currently zoned for urban purposes and generally served by utilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iii): at least 50% of the parcels within the survey area contain nonagricultural or nonaccessory buildings or improvements used or intended for residential, commercial, industrial, or other urban purposes;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv): the present condition or use of the survey area substantially impairs the sound growth of the community, delays the provision of housing accommodations, constitutes an economic liability, or is detrimental to the public health, safety, or welfare, as shown by the existence within the survey area of at least four of the following factors:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(A): although sometimes interspersed with well maintained buildings and infrastructure, substantial physical dilapidation, deterioration, or defective construction of buildings or infrastructure, or significant noncompliance with current building code, safety code, health code, or fire code requirements or local ordinances;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(B): unsanitary or unsafe conditions in the survey area that threaten the health, safety, or welfare of the community;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(C): environmental hazards, as defined in state or federal law, which require remediation as a condition for current or future use and development;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(D): excessive vacancy, abandoned buildings, or vacant lots within an area zoned for urban use and served by utilities;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(E): abandoned or outdated facilities that pose a threat to public health, safety, or welfare;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(F): criminal activity in the survey area, higher than that of comparable areas in the municipality or county that are without a development impediment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(iv)(G): defective or unusual conditions of title rendering the title nonmarketable; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(v): (1)(a)(iv)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(v)(A): (1)(a)(iv) at least 50% of the privately owned parcels within the survey area are affected by at least one of the factors, but not necessarily the same factor, listed in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(a)(v)(B): the affected parcels comprise at least 66% of the privately owned acreage within the survey area; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(b): 19-6-102 the survey area includes some or all of:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(b)(i): a superfund site;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(b)(ii): 19-6-102 a site used for the disposal of solid waste or hazardous waste, as those terms are defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(b)(iii): an inactive industrial site; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(1)(b)(iv): an inactive airport site.
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(2): (1)(a)(iii); (iv) A single parcel comprising 10% or more of the acreage within the survey area may not be counted as satisfying the requirement described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(3): (3)(b); (1); (1)(a)(iv); (3)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-405(3)(a): (3)(b); (1); (1)(a)(iv) Except as provided in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406 Challenging a finding of development impediment determination -- Time limit -- Standards governing court review.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(1): 17C-5-402(2)(c)(ii) If a board makes a development impediment determination under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2): 10-9a-801(3) In an action under this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(a): the agency shall transmit to the district court the record of the agency's proceedings, including any minutes, findings, determinations, orders, or transcripts of the agency's proceedings;
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(b): 10-9a-801(3) the district court shall review the development impediment determination under the standards of review provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(c): 
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(c)(i): if there is a record:
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(c)(i)(A): the district court's review is limited to the record provided by the agency; and
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(c)(i)(B): the district court may not accept or consider any evidence outside the record of the agency, unless the evidence was offered to the agency and the district court determines that the agency improperly excluded the evidence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 17C-5-406(2)(c)(ii): if there is no record, the district court may call witnesses and take evidence.
